PART I : SECTION (I)  — GENERAL 
 
Government  Notifications 
1A - PG 5729 — 1710 (01/2022)  
SRI   LANKA   INSTITUTE   OF   ARCHITECTS 
 
NEW Registration and Renewal of Registration of “Chartered Architects”, “Architects” and “Architectural Licentiates” 
for the year 2022/2023 under the Architects Registration Board,  established as per the Sri Lanka Institute of Architects 
(Amendment) Act, No. 14 of 1996. 
 
Reference is made to the notes appearing on pages 1A, 2A, 3A, 4A and 5A of the Gazette Extraordinary  
No.1015/19 of Friday, the 20 th February, 1998 of the Democratic Socialist Republic of Sri Lanka with regard to the 
Registration of persons who are eligible to practice Arch itecture in Sri Lanka under the Categories “Chartered 
Architects”, “Architects” and “Architect ural Licentiates”. The interpretations of the Sri Lanka Institute of Architects 
(Amendment) Act, No. 14 of 1996 in the above Gazette Notification will apply in all respects to the list published below. 
 
The Architects Registration Board of the Sri Lanka Institute of Architects as per the functions and powers 
vested upon it by the said Act. of Parliament, has now prepar ed the list of the “Chartered Architects”, “Architects” and 
“Architectural Licentiates” who are eligible to be Gazetted for the Year 2022/2023 (01 st February 2022 to 31 st January 
2023). 
The Architects Registration Board dir ected me to publish the Names, Ad dresses and Registration Numbers of 
the “Chartered Architects”, “Architects” and “Architectural Licentiates” who have been registered as given below.This 
registration expires on 31st January 2023. 
 
 
 N.W.W. WIJEKOON, 
 Registrar, 
 Architects Registration Board, 
 Sri Lanka Institute of Architects. 
 
No. 120/7, Vidya Mawatha, 
Colombo 07,  
24
th January 2022.
